{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01GzFiEs5c9ozSg8VXhrTFVy","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→//! `similar-asserts` is a crate that enhances the default assertion\n     2→//! experience by using [similar](https://crates.io/crates/similar) for diffing.\n     3→//! On failed assertions it renders out a colorized diff to the terminal.\n     4→//!\n     5→//! It comes with a handful of macros to replace [`std::assert_eq!`] with:\n     6→//!\n     7→//! - [`assert_eq!`]: diffs `Debug` on assertion failure.\n     8→#![cfg_attr(\n     9→    feature = \"serde\",\n    10→    doc = r#\"\n    11→- [`assert_serde_eq!`]: diffs `Serialize` on assertion failure.\n    12→\"#\n    13→)]\n    14→//!\n    15→//! ![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mitsuhiko/similar-asserts/main/assets/screenshot.png)\n    16→//!\n    17→//! # Usage\n    18→//!\n    19→//! ```rust\n    20→//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n    21→//! assert_eq!((1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>(), vec![1, 2]);\n    22→//! ```\n    23→//!\n    24→//! Optionally the assertion macros also let you \"name\" the left and right\n    25→//! side which will produce slightly more explicit output:\n    26→//!\n    27→//! ```rust\n    28→//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n    29→//! assert_eq!(expected: vec![1, 2], actual: (1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>());\n    30→//! ```\n    31→//!\n    32→//! # Feature Flags\n    33→//!\n    34→//! * `unicode` enable improved character matching (enabled by default)\n    35→//! * `serde` turns on support for serde.\n    36→//!\n    37→//! # Faster Builds\n    38→//!\n    39→//! This crate works best if you add it as `dev-dependency` only.  To make your code\n    40→//! still compile you can use conditional uses that override the default uses for the\n    41→//! `assert_eq!` macro from the stdlib:\n    42→//!\n    43→//! ```\n    44→//! #[cfg(test)]\n    45→//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n    46→//! ```\n    47→//!\n    48→//! Since `similar_asserts` uses the `similar` library for diffing you can also\n    49→//! enable optimziation for them in all build types for quicker diffing.  Add\n    50→//! this to your `Cargo.toml`:\n    51→//!\n    52→//! ```toml\n    53→//! [profile.dev.package.similar]\n    54→//! opt-level = 3\n    55→//! ```\n    56→//!\n    57→//! # String Truncation\n    58→//!\n    59→//! By default the assertion only shows 200 characters.  This can be changed with the\n    60→//! `SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH` environment variable.  Setting it to `0` disables\n    61→//! all truncation, otherwise it sets the maximum number of characters before truncation\n    62→//! kicks in.\n    63→//!\n    64→//! # Manual Diff Printing\n    65→//!\n    66→//! If you want to build your own comparison macros and you need a quick and simple\n    67→//! way to render diffs, you can use the [`SimpleDiff`] type and display it:\n    68→//!\n    69→//! ```should_panic\n    70→//! use similar_asserts::SimpleDiff;\n    71→//! panic!(\"Not equal\\n\\n{}\", SimpleDiff::from_str(\"a\\nb\\n\", \"b\\nb\\n\", \"left\", \"right\"));\n    72→//! ```\n    73→use std::borrow::Cow;\n    74→use std::fmt::{self, Display};\n    75→use std::time::Duration;\n    76→\n    77→use console::{style, Style};\n    78→use similar::{Algorithm, ChangeTag, TextDiff};\n    79→\n    80→#[cfg(feature = \"serde\")]\n    81→#[doc(hidden)]\n    82→pub mod serde_impl;\n    83→\n    84→// This needs to be public as we are using it internally in a macro.\n    85→#[doc(hidden)]\n    86→pub mod print;\n    87→\n    88→/// The maximum number of characters a string can be long before truncating.\n    89→fn get_max_string_length() -> usize {\n    90→    use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering};\n    91→    static TRUNCATE: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(!0);\n    92→    let rv = TRUNCATE.load(Ordering::Relaxed);\n    93→    if rv != !0 {\n    94→        return rv;\n    95→    }\n    96→    let rv: usize = std::env::var(\"SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH\")\n    97→        .ok()\n    98→        .and_then(|x| x.parse().ok())\n    99→        .unwrap_or(200);\n   100→    TRUNCATE.store(rv, Ordering::Relaxed);\n   101→    rv\n   102→}\n   103→\n   104→/// A console printable diff.\n   105→///\n   106→/// The [`Display`](std::fmt::Display) implementation of this type renders out a\n   107→/// diff with ANSI markers so it creates a nice colored diff. This can be used to\n   108→/// build your own custom assertions in addition to the ones from this crate.\n   109→///\n   110→/// It does not provide much customization beyond what's possible done by default.\n   111→pub struct SimpleDiff<'a> {\n   112→    pub(crate) left_short: Cow<'a, str>,\n   113→    pub(crate) right_short: Cow<'a, str>,\n   114→    pub(crate) left_expanded: Option<Cow<'a, str>>,\n   115→    pub(crate) right_expanded: Option<Cow<'a, str>>,\n   116→    pub(crate) left_label: &'a str,\n   117→    pub(crate) right_label: &'a str,\n   118→}\n   119→\n   120→impl<'a> SimpleDiff<'a> {\n   121→    /// Creates a diff from two strings.\n   122→    ///\n   123→    /// `left_label` and `right_label` are the labels used for the two sides.\n   124→    /// `\"left\"` and On failed assertions it renders out a colorized diff to the terminal.\n//!\n//! It comes with a handful of macros to replace [`std::assert_eq!`] with:\n//!\n//! - [`assert_eq!`]: diffs `Debug` on assertion failure.\n#![cfg_attr(\n    feature = \"serde\",\n    doc = r#\"\n- [`assert_serde_eq!`]: diffs `Serialize` on assertion failure.\n\"#\n)]\n//!\n//! ![](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/mitsuhiko/similar-asserts/main/assets/screenshot.png)\n//!\n//! # Usage\n//!\n//! ```rust\n//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n//! assert_eq!((1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>(), vec![1, 2]);\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Optionally the assertion macros also let you \"name\" the left and right\n//! side which will produce slightly more explicit output:\n//!\n//! ```rust\n//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n//! assert_eq!(expected: vec![1, 2], actual: (1..3).collect::<Vec<_>>());\n//! ```\n//!\n//! # Feature Flags\n//!\n//! * `unicode` enable improved character matching (enabled by default)\n//! * `serde` turns on support for serde.\n//!\n//! # Faster Builds\n//!\n//! This crate works best if you add it as `dev-dependency` only.  To make your code\n//! still compile you can use conditional uses that override the default uses for the\n//! `assert_eq!` macro from the stdlib:\n//!\n//! ```\n//! #[cfg(test)]\n//! use similar_asserts::assert_eq;\n//! ```\n//!\n//! Since `similar_asserts` uses the `similar` library for diffing you can also\n//! enable optimziation for them in all build types for quicker diffing.  Add\n//! this to your `Cargo.toml`:\n//!\n//! ```toml\n//! [profile.dev.package.similar]\n//! opt-level = 3\n//! ```\n//!\n//! # String Truncation\n//!\n//! By default the assertion only shows 200 characters.  This can be changed with the\n//! `SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH` environment variable.  Setting it to `0` disables\n//! all truncation, otherwise it sets the maximum number of characters before truncation\n//! kicks in.\n//!\n//! # Manual Diff Printing\n//!\n//! If you want to build your own comparison macros and you need a quick and simple\n//! way to render diffs, you can use the [`SimpleDiff`] type and display it:\n//!\n//! ```should_panic\n//! use similar_asserts::SimpleDiff;\n//! panic!(\"Not equal\\n\\n{}\", SimpleDiff::from_str(\"a\\nb\\n\", \"b\\nb\\n\", \"left\", \"right\"));\n//! ```\nuse std::borrow::Cow;\nuse std::fmt::{self, Display};\nuse std::time::Duration;\n\nuse console::{style, Style};\nuse similar::{Algorithm, ChangeTag, TextDiff};\n\n#[cfg(feature = \"serde\")]\n#[doc(hidden)]\npub mod serde_impl;\n\n// This needs to be public as we are using it internally in a macro.\n#[doc(hidden)]\npub mod print;\n\n/// The maximum number of characters a string can be long before truncating.\nfn get_max_string_length() -> usize {\n    use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicUsize, Ordering};\n    static TRUNCATE: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(!0);\n    let rv = TRUNCATE.load(Ordering::Relaxed);\n    if rv != !0 {\n        return rv;\n    }\n    let rv: usize = std::env::var(\"SIMILAR_ASSERTS_MAX_STRING_LENGTH\")\n        .ok()\n        .and_then(|x| x.parse().ok())\n        .unwrap_or(200);\n    TRUNCATE.store(rv, Ordering::Relaxed);\n    rv\n}\n\n/// A console printable diff.\n///\n/// The [`Display`](std::fmt::Display) implementation of this type renders out a\n/// diff with ANSI markers so it creates a nice colored diff. detected_lf)\n}\n\n#[allow(clippy::match_like_matches_macro)]\nfn newlines_matter(left: &str, right: &str) -> bool {\n    if trailing_newline(left) != trailing_newline(right) {\n        return true;\n    }\n\n    let (cr1, crlf1, lf1) = detect_newlines(left);\n    let (cr2, crlf2, lf2) = detect_newlines(right);\n\n    match (cr1 || cr2, crlf1 || crlf2, lf1 || lf2) {\n        (false, false, false) => false,\n        (true, false, false) => false,\n        (false, true, false) => false,\n        (false, false, true) => false,\n        _ => true,\n    }\n}\n\nimpl<'a> fmt::Display for SimpleDiff<'a> {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter) -> fmt::Result {\n        let left = self.left();\n        let right = self.right();\n        let newlines_matter = newlines_matter(left, right);\n\n        if left == right {\n            writeln!(\n                f,\n                \"{}: the two values are the same in string form.\",\n                style(\"Invisible differences\").bold(),\n            )?;\n            return Ok(());\n        }\n\n        let diff = TextDiff::configure()\n            .timeout(Duration::from_millis(200))\n            .algorithm(Algorithm::Patience)\n            .diff_lines(left, right);\n\n        writeln!(\n            f,\n            \"{} ({}{}|{}{}):\",\n            style(\"Differences\").bold(),\n diff.grouped_ops(4).into_iter().enumerate() {\n            if idx > 0 {\n                writeln!(f, \"@ {}\", style(\"~~~\").dim())?;\n            }\n            for op in group {\n        ChangeTag::Insert => ('+', Style::new().green()),\n                        ChangeTag::Equal => (' ', Style::new().dim()),\n                    };\n                    write!(f, \"{}\",                  .replace(\"␍\\r␊\\n\", \"␍␊\\r\\n\"),\n                            )\n                        } else {\n                            Cow::Borrowed(value)\n                        };\n    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n#[doc(hidden)]\n#[macro_export]\nmacro_rules! __assert_eq {\n    (\n        $method:ident,\n
